&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;  &lt;p&gt;&lt;span style="color: black;"&gt;&amp;nbsp; }&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;  &lt;p&gt;&lt;span style="color: black;"&gt;}&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;  &lt;p&gt;&lt;span style="color: black;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;  &lt;p&gt;&lt;span style="color: black;"&gt;public class Tester&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;  &lt;p&gt;&lt;span style="color: black;"&gt;{&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;  &lt;p&gt;&lt;span style="color: black;"&gt;&amp;nbsp; <p><span style="color: black;">Fill in the blanks so that the following draws a Frame containing "Hello".</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">import java.awt.*; </span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">class helloFrame ___________ Frame</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">{</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp; public void ___________( Graphics g )</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp; {</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; g.___________("Hello", 10, 50 );&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp; }</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">}</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">public class Tester</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">{</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp; public static void main ( String[] args )</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp; {</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; helloFrame frm = new helloFrame();&nbsp; </span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; frm.setSize( 150, 100 ); </span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; frm.setVisible( true );</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp; }</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">}</span></p>  <p><br></p>

<p><span style="color: black;">What will be the output of the following program?</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">public class BlockFinal</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">{</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; public static void main(String[] a)</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; {</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; try</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; {</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; int i = 10 / 0;</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; }</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; catch (Exception ex)</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; {</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; System.out.println("1st catch Block");</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; }</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; finally</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; {</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; System.out.println("1st finally block");</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; }</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; try</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; {</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; int i = 10 / 10;</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; }</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; catch (Exception ex)</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; {</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; System.out.println("2nd catch Block");</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; }</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; finally</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; {</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;System.out.println("2nd finally block");</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; }</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; }</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">}</span></p>  <p><br></p>

        <textarea disabled="" style="display: none;" name="question_text" class="textarea_question_text">Which of the following ways can be used to handle exceptions? X: By wrapping the desired code in a try block followed by a catch block to catch the exceptions. Y: List the desired exceptions in the throws clause of the method and let the caller of the method handle those exceptions.</textarea>
      </div>
      <div id="question_16788196_question_text" class="question_text user_content enhanced">
          Which of the following ways can be used to handle exceptions? X: By wrapping the desired code in a try block followed by a catch block to catch the exceptions. Y: List the desired exceptions in the throws clause of the method and let the caller of the method handle those exceptions.
      </div>
      <div class="answers">
                <div class="answers_wrapper">
                  
    <div class="answer answer_for_
         
         
         
         
         selected_answer unspecified_answer" id="answer_27243" style="" title="Both X and Y. You selected this answer.">


      <span class="hidden id">27243</span>

    <div class="select_answer answer_type">
        <input id="answer-27243" name="question-16788196" type="radio" checked="" class="question_input" aria-disabled="true" disabled="" wfd-id="id84">&nbsp;
      <label for="answer-27243">
        <div class="answer_text">Both X and Y</div>
        <div class="answer_html"></div>
      </label>

<p><span style="font-family: &quot;Andale Mono&quot;; color: black;">What will happen when you compile and run the following code?</span></p>  <p><span style="font-family: &quot;Andale Mono&quot;; color: black;">&nbsp;</span></p>  <p><span style="font-family: &quot;Andale Mono&quot;; color: black;">public class Test{&nbsp; </span></p>  <p><span style="font-family: &quot;Andale Mono&quot;; color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></p>  <p><span style="font-family: &quot;Andale Mono&quot;; color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; public static void main(String[] args){</span></p>  <p><span style="font-family: &quot;Andale Mono&quot;; color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; try{</span></p>  <p><span style="font-family: &quot;Andale Mono&quot;; color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; if(t.className.equals("Test"))</span></p>  <p><span style="font-family: &quot;Andale Mono&quot;; color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;       <div id="question_16826891_question_text" class="question_text user_content enhanced">
          
<p><span style="color: black;">What will happen when you compile and run the following code with assertion enabled?</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">public class Test{</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; public static void main(String[] args){</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; int[] marks = {40, 38, 52}; </span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; boolean[] pass = {false, false, false};</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; for(int i = 0 ; i &lt; marks.length; i++){</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; try{</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; assert marks[i] &gt;= 40 : pass[i] = true;</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; }catch(AssertionError ae){</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; pass[i] = false;</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;  &lt;p&gt;&lt;span style="color: black;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; {&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;  &lt;p&gt;&lt;span style="color: black;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; return y * 2;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;  &lt;p&gt;&lt;span style="color: black;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; }&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;  &lt;p&gt;&lt;span style="color: black;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; public static void main(String [] args) &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;  &lt;p&gt;&lt;span style="color: black;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; {&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;  &lt;p&gt;&lt;span style="color: black;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; int z = 5;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;  &lt;p&gt;&lt;span style="color: black;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; assert z &amp;gt; 0; /* Line 11 */&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;  &lt;p&gt;&lt;span style="color: black;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; assert z &amp;gt; 2: foo(z); /* Line 12 */&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;  &lt;p&gt;&lt;span style="color: black;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; if ( z &amp;lt; 7 )&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;  &lt;p&gt;&lt;span style="color: black;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; assert z &amp;gt; 4; /* Line 14 */&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;  &lt;p&gt;&lt;span style="color: black;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;  &lt;p&gt;&lt;span style="color: black;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; switch (z) &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;  &lt;p&gt;&lt;span style="color: black;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; {&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;  &lt;p&gt;&lt;span style="color: black;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; case 4: System.out.println("4 ");&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;  &lt;p&gt;&lt;span style="color: black;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; case 5: System.out.println("5 ");&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;  &lt;p&gt;&lt;span style="color: black;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; default: assert z &amp;lt; 10;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;  &lt;p&gt;&lt;span style="color: black;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; }&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;  &lt;p&gt;&lt;span style="color: black;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;  &lt;p&gt;&lt;span style="color: black;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; if ( z &amp;lt; 10 )&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;  &lt;p&gt;&lt;span style="color: black;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; assert z &amp;gt; 4: z++; /* Line 22 */&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;  &lt;p&gt;&lt;span style="color: black;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; System.out.println(z);&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;  &lt;p&gt;&lt;span style="color: black;"&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp; }&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;  &lt;p&gt;&lt;span style="color: black;"&gt;}&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;  &lt;p&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Calibri , sans-serif; color: black;"&gt;which line is an example of an inappropriate use of assertions?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
</textarea>
      </div>
      <div id="question_16777510_question_text" class="question_text user_content enhanced">
          
<p><span style="color: black;">public class Test2 </span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">{</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; public static int x;</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; public static int foo(int y) </span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; {</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; return y * 2;</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; }</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; public static void main(String [] args) </span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; {</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; int z = 5;</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; assert z &gt; 0; /* Line 11 */</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; assert z &gt; 2: foo(z); /* Line 12 */</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; if ( z &lt; 7 )</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; assert z &gt; 4; /* Line 14 */</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; switch (z) </span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; {</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; case 4: System.out.println("4 ");</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; case 5: System.out.println("5 ");</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; default: assert z &lt; 10;</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; }</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; if ( z &lt; 10 )</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; assert z &gt; 4: z++; /* Line 22 */</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; System.out.println(z);</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; }</span></p>  <p><span style="color: black;">}</span></p>  <p><span style="font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Calibri , sans-serif; color: black;">which line is an example of an inappropriate use of assertions?</span></p>

      </div>
